# product/search/param/group

- request: https://wmsc.lcsc.com/wmsc/product/search/param/group
- method: POST
- body (raw):
```json
{
    "brandIdList": [],
    "catalogIdList": [
        308
    ],
    "isStock": false,
    "isEnvironment": false,
    "isHot": false,
    "isDiscount": false,
    "encapValueList": [],
    "paramNameValueMap": {}
}
```
